namespace = ztr_decolonization

# Main Decolonization Event Template
ztr_decolonization.1 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_war_civilians"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.1.t
	desc = ztr_decolonization.1.d
	flavor = ztr_decolonization.1.f

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		# Fired via on_action only; no self-trigger
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.1.a
		default_option = yes
	}
}

# Tunisia Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.2 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.2.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.2.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.2.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.2.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_tunisia = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_tunisia_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:maghrebi = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.2.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_tunisia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:TUN months = 120 }
		c:TUN = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.2.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:maghrebi = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_tunisia_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_tunisia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:TUN months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:TUN type = colony }
		c:TUN = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:maghrebi = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:TUN = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:maghrebi = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_tunisia = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:TUN type = colony }
		c:TUN = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_tunisia_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Algeria Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.3 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "votp_french_algeria"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.3.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.3.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.3.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.3.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_algeria = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_algeria_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:maghrebi = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.3.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_algeria = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ALD months = 120 }
		c:ALD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.3.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:maghrebi = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_algeria_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
					NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
				}
				AND = { c:FRA ?= this }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_algeria = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ALD months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ALD type = colony }
		c:ALD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:maghrebi = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ALD = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:maghrebi = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_algeria = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ALD type = colony }
		c:ALD = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_algeria_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

	dlc = dlc_tech_res

# Egypt Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.6 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }

		video = "middleeast_police_breaking_door"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "middleeast_courtroom_upheaval"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.6.t

		c:EGY = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:misri = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:EGY = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:misri = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_egypt = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:EGY type = colony }
		c:EGY = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_egypt_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}

# Sudan Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.7 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.7.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.7.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.7.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.7.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_sudan = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_sudan_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:sudanese = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.7.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_sudan = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:SUD months = 120 }
		c:SUD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.7.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:sudanese = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_sudan_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_sudan = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:SUD months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:SUD type = colony }
		c:SUD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:sudanese = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:SUD = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:sudanese = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_sudan = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:SUD type = colony }
		c:SUD = {

				type = dp_independence
			}
		}

	}

# Trucial States Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.11 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "middleeast_police_breaking_door"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "middleeast_courtroom_upheaval"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.11.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.11.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.11.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.11.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_trucial_states = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_trucial_states_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:bedouin = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.11.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:BHN } }
			create_country = {
				tag = BHN
				origin = this
				province = p:x505AE0
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:ABU } }
			create_country = {
				tag = ABU
				origin = this
				province = p:x65a581
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
					any_scope_state = { owner = ROOT }
				}
			}
			s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
				set_owner_of_provinces = {
					country = c:BHN
					provinces = { x505AE0 x2768F8 xEF5020 }
				}
				random_scope_state = {
					limit = { owner = root }
					set_state_owner = c:ABU
				}
			}
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:BHN months = 120 }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ABU months = 120 }
		c:BHN = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
		c:ABU = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.11.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:bedouin = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_trucial_states_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:BHN } }
			create_country = {
				tag = BHN
				origin = this
				province = p:x505AE0
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:ABU } }
			create_country = {
				tag = ABU
				origin = this
				province = p:x65a581
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
					any_scope_state = { owner = ROOT }
				}
			}
			s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
				set_owner_of_provinces = {
					country = c:BHN
					provinces = { x505AE0 x2768F8 xEF5020 }
				}
				random_scope_state = {
					limit = { owner = root }
					set_state_owner = c:ABU
				}
			}
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:BHN months = 120 }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ABU months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:BHN type = colony }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ABU type = colony }
		c:BHN = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		c:ABU = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:bedouin = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:BHN = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:bedouin = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:BHN } }
			create_country = {
				tag = BHN
				origin = this
				province = p:x505AE0
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:ABU } }
			create_country = {
				tag = ABU
				origin = this
				province = p:x65a581
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
					any_scope_state = { owner = ROOT }
				}
			}
			s:STATE_ABU_DHABI = {
				set_owner_of_provinces = {
					country = c:BHN
					provinces = { x505AE0 x2768F8 xEF5020 }
				}
				random_scope_state = {
					limit = { owner = root }
					set_state_owner = c:ABU
				}
			}
		}
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:BHN type = colony }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ABU type = colony }
		c:BHN = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_trucial_states_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Persia Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.12 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "middleeast_police_breaking_door"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "votp_gunboat_diplomacy"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.12.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.12.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.12.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.12.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_persia = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_persia_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:persian = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.12.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_persia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:PER months = 120 }
		c:PER = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.12.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:persian = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_persia_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_persia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:PER months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:PER type = colony }
		c:PER = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:persian = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:PER = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:persian = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_persia = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:PER type = colony }
		c:PER = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_persia_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		}

		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:LAO type = colony }
		c:LAO = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_laos_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Vietnam Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.16 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "asia_sepoy_mutiny"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "asia_union_leader"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "asia_politician_parliament_motion"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.16.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.16.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.16.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.16.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_vietnam = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_vietnam_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:vietnamese = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.16.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_vietnam = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:DAI months = 120 }
		c:DAI = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.16.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:vietnamese = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_vietnam_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_vietnam = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:DAI months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:DAI type = colony }
		c:DAI = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:vietnamese = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:DAI = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:vietnamese = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_vietnam = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:DAI type = colony }
		c:DAI = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_vietnam_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

# India Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.18 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "ip2_unruly_soldiers"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "ip2_india_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "asia_politician_parliament_motion"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.18.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.18.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.18.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.18.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_india = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_india_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = c:BHT
			}
			c:BHT = { save_scope_as = ztr_indian_unifier_scope }
		}
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.18.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_india
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_CEYLON }
			}
			set_state_owner = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_europe }
			create_bidirectional_truce = { country = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope months = 120 }
		}
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.18.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_india_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_india
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_CEYLON }
			}
			set_state_owner = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope
		}
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope type = colony }
		scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_india
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_CEYLON }
			}
			set_state_owner = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope
		}
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope type = colony }
		scope:ztr_indian_unifier_scope = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_india_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		c:JAP = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:japanese = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_japan = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:JAP type = colony }
		c:JAP = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_japan_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# China Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.21 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "votp_barricade"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "asia_union_leader"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "votp_gunboat_diplomacy"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.21.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.21.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.21.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.21.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_china = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_china_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:han = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.21.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = sr:region_north_china
					region = sr:region_south_china
				}
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_SHAOZHOU }
			}
			set_state_owner = c:CHI
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:CHI months = 120 }
		c:CHI = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.21.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:han = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_china_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = sr:region_north_china
					region = sr:region_south_china
				}
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_SHAOZHOU }
			}
			set_state_owner = c:CHI
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:CHI months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:CHI type = colony }
		c:CHI = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:han = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:CHI = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:han = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = sr:region_north_china
					region = sr:region_south_china
				}
				NOT = { state_region = s:STATE_SHAOZHOU }
			}
			set_state_owner = c:CHI
		}
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:CHI type = colony }
		c:CHI = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_china_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_bhutan = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:BHU months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:BHU type = colony }
		c:BHU = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:tibetan = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:BHU = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:tibetan = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_bhutan = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:BHU type = colony }
		c:BHU = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_bhutan_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}

	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.26.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.26.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.26.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_tibet = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_tibet_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:tibetan = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.26.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }

		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }

			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_tibet = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:TIB months = 120 }
		c:TIB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.26.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:tibetan = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_tibet_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_tibet = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:TIB months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:TIB type = colony }
		c:TIB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:tibetan = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:TIB = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:tibetan = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }

		c:LEB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:LEB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.30.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:mashriqi = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_lebanon_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_lebanon = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:LEB months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:LEB type = colony }
		c:LEB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:LEB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:mashriqi = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:LEB = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:mashriqi = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_lebanon = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:LEB type = colony }
		c:LEB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:LEB = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_lebanon_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.35.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.35.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.35.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.35.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_namibia = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_namibia_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:khoisan = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.35.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_namibia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNB months = 120 }
		c:ZNB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.35.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:khoisan = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_namibia_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_namibia = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNB months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNB type = colony }
		c:ZNB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNB = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:khoisan = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZNB = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:khoisan = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_namibia = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNB type = colony }
		c:ZNB = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNB = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_namibia_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		}
		ztr_define_niger = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NIGER } s:STATE_NIGER = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNI } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNI months = 120 }
		c:ZNI = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }

		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:equatorial_bantu = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_niger_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }

		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_niger = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NIGER } s:STATE_NIGER = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNI } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNI months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNI type = colony }
		c:ZNI = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNI = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:equatorial_bantu = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZNI = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:equatorial_bantu = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_niger = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NIGER } s:STATE_NIGER = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNI } } }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNI type = colony }
		c:ZNI = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNI = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_niger_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Mauritania Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.40 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.40.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.40.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.40.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.40.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_mauritania = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_mauritania_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:bidan = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.40.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_mauritania = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZMU months = 120 }
		c:ZMU = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZMU = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.40.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:bidan = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_mauritania_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_mauritania = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZMU months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZMU type = colony }
		c:ZMU = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZMU = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:bidan = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZMU = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:bidan = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_mauritania = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZMU type = colony }
		c:ZMU = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZMU = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_mauritania_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		ztr_define_ghana = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZGH months = 120 }
		c:ZGH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZGH = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.44.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:akan = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_ghana_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_ghana = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZGH months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZGH type = colony }
		c:ZGH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZGH = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:akan = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZGH = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:akan = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_ghana = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZGH type = colony }
		c:ZGH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZGH = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_ghana_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND } s:STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNG months = 120 }

			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }

			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }

		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BORNU } s:STATE_BORNU = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND } s:STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZNG months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNG type = colony }
		c:ZNG = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNG = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:yoruba = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZNG = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:yoruba = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_nigeria = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NIGERIA } s:STATE_NIGERIA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_YORUBA_STATES } s:STATE_YORUBA_STATES = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NIGER_DELTA } s:STATE_NIGER_DELTA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BORNU } s:STATE_BORNU = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND } s:STATE_EAST_HAUSALAND = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZNG } } }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZNG type = colony }
		c:ZNG = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZNG = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_nigeria_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Cameroon Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.49 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.49.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.49.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.49.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.49.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_cameroon = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_cameroon_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:fulbe = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.49.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_camerun = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZCM months = 120 }
		c:ZCM = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZCM = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.49.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:fulbe = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_cameroon_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_camerun = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZCM months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZCM type = colony }
		c:ZCM = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZCM = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:fulbe = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZCM = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:fulbe = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_camerun = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_SOUTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON } s:STATE_NORTH_CAMEROON = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZCM } } }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZCM type = colony }
		c:ZCM = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZCM = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_cameroon_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_republic_of_the_congo = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZCG type = colony }
		c:ZCG = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZCG = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_republic_of_the_congo_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# DR Congo Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.53 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.53.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.53.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.53.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.53.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_dr_congo = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_dr_congo_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:fluvian_bantu = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.53.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_democratic_republic_of_the_congo = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZDC months = 120 }
		c:ZDC = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZDC = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.53.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:fluvian_bantu = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_dr_congo_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_democratic_republic_of_the_congo = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZDC months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZDC type = colony }
		c:ZDC = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZDC = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:fluvian_bantu = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZDC = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:fluvian_bantu = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_democratic_republic_of_the_congo = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZDC type = colony }
		c:ZDC = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZDC = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_dr_congo_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:kavango_bantu = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_angola_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_angola = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZAG months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZAG type = colony }
		c:ZAG = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZAG = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:kavango_bantu = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZAG = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:kavango_bantu = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_angola = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZAG type = colony }
		c:ZAG = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZAG = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_angola_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_zambia = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_zambia_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:lunda = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

		c:ZZM = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZZM = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }

			change_infamy = 5
		}

			change_infamy = 3

			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }

		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_mozambique = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_mozambique_decolonization_cd }

	}

			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_mozambico = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LOURENCO_MARQUES } s:STATE_LOURENCO_MARQUES = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZMZ } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZMZ months = 120 }
		c:ZMZ = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }

	}

		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:sena = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_mozambique_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {

		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_mozambico = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LOURENCO_MARQUES } s:STATE_LOURENCO_MARQUES = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZMZ } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZMZ months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZMZ type = colony }
		c:ZMZ = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZMZ = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:sena = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZMZ = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }

			cu:sena = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }

		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.62.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.62.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.62.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.62.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_lesotho = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_lesotho_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:sotho = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.62.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_lesotho = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZUL months = 120 }
		c:ZUL = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZUL = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.62.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:sotho = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_lesotho_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_lesotho = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZUL months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZUL type = colony }
		c:ZUL = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZUL = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:sotho = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ZUL = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:sotho = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_lesotho = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZUL type = colony }
		c:ZUL = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ZUL = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_lesotho_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)

		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }

		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = c:ZBT } }
			create_country = {
				tag = ZBT
				origin = this
				province = p:x958940
				on_created = {
					set_country_type = recognized
					activate_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
					activate_law = law_type:law_census_voting
					activate_law = law_type:law_no_schools
				}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BOTSWANA } s:STATE_BOTSWANA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZBT } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ZBT months = 120 }
		c:ZBT = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }

		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}

			change_infamy = 3
		}

	}

			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {

			change_infamy = -2
		}

			create_country = {
				tag = ZBT
				origin = this
				province = p:x958940

					activate_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
					activate_law = law_type:law_census_voting
					activate_law = law_type:law_no_schools
				}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BOTSWANA } s:STATE_BOTSWANA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ZBT } } }

		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ZBT type = colony }
