			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_zimbabwe_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
# Madagascar Decolonization
ztr_decolonization.66 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
		video = "africa_soldiers_breaking_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.66.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.66.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.66.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.66.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_madagascar = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_madagascar_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:malagasy = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.66.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_madagascar = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:MAD months = 120 }
		c:MAD = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:MAD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.66.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:malagasy = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_madagascar_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_madagascar = yes
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:MAD months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:MAD type = colony }
		c:MAD = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:MAD = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:malagasy = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:MAD = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:malagasy = { fervor >= 60 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_madagascar = yes
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:MAD type = colony }
		c:MAD = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:MAD = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_independence
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_madagascar_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}

		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}

	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.67.d_phase4 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.67.d_phase3 }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { always = yes } desc = ztr_decolonization.67.d_phase2 }
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		ztr_can_decolonize_ethiopia = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_ethiopia_decolonization_cd }
	}

	immediate = {
		cu:amhara = { save_scope_as = ztr_decolonization_culture_scope }
	}

	# Option A: Grant Independence (Phase 3+)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.67.a
		trigger = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -5
		}
		ztr_define_ethiopia = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ERITREA } s:STATE_ERITREA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ETH } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ETH months = 120 }
		c:ETH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ETH = { change_relations = { country = root value = 50 } }
	}

	# Option B: Reject Independence (Not Phase 3)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.67.b
		trigger = { NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes } }
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_increase_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = 5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		cu:amhara = { add_fervor = 15 }
		set_variable = { name = ztr_ethiopia_decolonization_cd years = 3 }
	}

	# Option C: Create as Colony
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes }
			country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			NOT = { any_subject_or_below = { count > 5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_5_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy > 10 }
			change_infamy = -2
		}
		ztr_define_ethiopia = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ERITREA } s:STATE_ERITREA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ETH } } }
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = c:ETH months = 120 }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ETH type = colony }
		c:ETH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ETH = { change_relations = { country = root value = 25 } }
		cu:amhara = { add_fervor = 20 }
		c:ETH = { set_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd years = 4 } }
	}

	# Option E: War of Independence (Phase 4 + high fervor)
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.e
		trigger = {
			ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
			cu:amhara = { fervor >= 50 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		custom_tooltip = ztr_decolonization_pressure_decrease_15_tt
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { name = ztr_decolonization_pressure_var add = -15 } }
		if = {
			limit = { infamy < 50 }
			change_infamy = 5
		}
		else = {
			change_infamy = 3
		}
		ztr_define_ethiopia = yes
		if = { limit = { has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ERITREA } s:STATE_ERITREA = { random_scope_state = { limit = { owner = root } set_state_owner = c:ETH } } }
		create_diplomatic_pact = { country = c:ETH type = colony }
		c:ETH = { add_journal_entry = { type = je_demographic_0_to_1 } }
		c:ETH = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				target_country = root
				type = dp_annex_war
			}
		}
		set_variable = { name = ztr_ethiopia_decolonization_cd years = 5 }
	}
}
###GENERAL DECOLONIZATION EVENT
# Winds of Decolonization (Phase 3-4)

# UN Decolonization Demand (Phase 4)
# UN has Encourage Decolonization Law and asks country with infamy above 10 to decolonize a subject
ztr_decolonization.101 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	event_image = {
		video = "un_foundation"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.101.t
	desc = ztr_decolonization.101.d

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = allow_ztr_decolonization_content
		has_global_variable = ztr_global_decolonization_pressure_var
		ztr_decolonization_is_phase_4 = yes
		ztr_is_un_member = yes
		has_global_variable = ztr_un_hr_decolonization
		global_var:ztr_un_hr_decolonization = 2
		infamy > 10
		NOT = { has_variable = ztr_un_decolonization_demand_cd }
		any_subject_or_below = {
			NOT = { is_subject_of = c:BIC }
			NOT = { c:BIC = root }
			NOT = { is_subject_of = c:DEI }
			NOT = { is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of = root }
			NOT = { has_variable = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ztr_un_decolonization_demand_cd
			years = 5
		}
		random_subject_or_below = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_subject_of = c:BIC }
				NOT = { c:BIC = root }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = c:DEI }
				NOT = { is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of = root }
				NOT = { has_variable = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd }
			}
			save_scope_as = un_demand_subject
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.101.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					ztr_is_full_democratic = yes
				}
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					ztr_is_democratic = yes
				}
				add = 15
			}
		}
		change_infamy = -5
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = scope:un_demand_subject months = 120 }
		scope:un_demand_subject = {
			make_independent = yes
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = 50
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.101.b
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		change_infamy = 5
		add_modifier = {
			name = ztr_un_condemned_modifier
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		scope:un_demand_subject = {
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -50
			}
		}
	}
}

ztr_decolonization.100 = {
	dlc = dlc_tech_res
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_europe }
		}
		video = "europenorthamerica_springtime_of_nations"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_north_africa }
		}
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_middle_east }
		}
		video = "middleeast_courtroom_upheaval"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_subsaharan_africa }
		}
		video = "africa_public_protest"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_india }
		}
		video = "ip2_india_protest"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_east_asia }
		}
		video = "ep1_donghak_rebellion"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = { is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_south_east_asia }
		}
		video = "asia_buddhism"

		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}
	event_image = {
		trigger = {
			scope:subject_scope = {
				NOR = {
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_europe
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_north_africa
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_middle_east
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_subsaharan_africa
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_india
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_east_asia
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_south_east_asia
				}
			}
		}
		video = "southamerica_war_civilians"
		on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/decolonization_event.dds"

	title = ztr_decolonization.100.t
	desc = ztr_decolonization.100.d


	duration = 3
	
	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = allow_ztr_decolonization_content
		has_global_variable = ztr_global_decolonization_pressure_var
		ztr_decolonization_is_phase_3 = yes
		any_subject_or_below = {
			#No decolonization events for british raj vassals, as they are too much and very annoying
			NOT = { is_subject_of = c:BIC}
			NOT = {	c:BIC = root }
			#No decolonization events for west indies vassals, as they are too much and very annoying
			NOT = { is_subject_of = c:DEI}
			NOT = {	is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of = root }
			NOT = {	has_variable = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd }
			liberty_desire > 90
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = decolonization_subject_event_var
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
			value = 0
		}
		random_subject_or_below = {
			limit = {
				#No decolonization events for british raj vassals, as they are too much and very annoying
				NOT = { is_subject_of = c:BIC}
				NOT = {	c:BIC = root }
				#No decolonization events for west indies vassals, as they are too much and very annoying
				NOT = { is_subject_of = c:DEI}
				NOT = {	is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of = root }
				NOT = {	has_variable = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd }
				liberty_desire > 90
			}
			save_scope_as = subject_scope
		}
		calculate_infamy_decolonization_subject_event = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
			value = var:decolonization_subject_event_var
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
			multiply = -1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.100.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			# 4:1 for full democracies, 2.5:1 for democracies and 1:1 for others
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					ztr_is_full_democratic = yes
				}
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					ztr_is_democratic = yes
				}
				add = 15
			}
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = { country = scope:subject_scope months = 120 }
		change_infamy = var:decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
		remove_variable = decolonization_subject_event_var
		remove_variable = decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
		scope:subject_scope = {
			make_independent = yes
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = 50
			}
		}
	}

	#TODO Rendere questo solo qualcosa per la phase 4
	option = {
		name = ztr_decolonization.100.b
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = scope:subject_scope
			value = var:decolonization_subject_event_var
		}
		remove_variable = decolonization_subject_event_var
		remove_variable = decolonization_subject_event_var_neg
		scope:subject_scope = {
			set_variable = {
				name = ztr_decolonization_subject_cd
				years = 5
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -100
			}
			create_diplomatic_play = {
			target_country = root
			type = dp_independence
		}
		}
	}

	#TODO Aggiungere opzione per fase 3 in cui non si scatena guerra civile ma aumenta decolonization pressure
}
